msg:I booked the Arcadia Hotel in Langfang on Ctrip. The check-in experience exceeded my expectations! Let me start with the service at the front desk. Since it was not a holiday and weekend, I was proactively upgraded from the suite in Building B to the deluxe suite in Building A for free, which really gave me a big surprise! The front desk also added my WeChat (her WeChat ID is hao), and enthusiastically introduced the performances and time of the Dream of Red Mansions Film and Television City that I was going to, which made me feel at home!
In addition, the hotel rooms are clean and sanitary, and there is a free parking lot at the door. It is also very close to the Dream of Red Mansions, with a superior geographical location and convenient transportation.
The hotel has a wide variety of breakfasts, including noodles, wontons, and pancakes. The Chinese restaurant is also very delicious with Shandong cuisine. The entire hotel has Wi-Fi, and the Internet speed in the room is very smooth. If you just want to have a quick meal, go out of the hotel gate and walk a short distance to the left. There is an Aka Kitchen. The 99 yuan double set meal not only has 4 dishes, but also comes with a liter of sour plum soup, which is enough for three people. In short, the software and hardware of Arcadia Five-Star Hotel are worthy of the name. It is a hotel worth recommending for business trips and travels to Langfang!
